class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/api"><span>APIs</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/api/graphql"><span>Search API - GraphQL/gRPC</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Conditional filters</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Conditional filters</h1></header>
<p>Conditional filters may be added to queries such as <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/get"><code>Object-level</code></a> and <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/aggregate"><code>Aggregate</code></a> queries, as well as <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-objects/delete#delete-multiple-objects">batch deletion</a>. The operator used for filtering is also called a <code>where</code> filter.</p>
<p>A filter may consist of one or more conditions, which are combined using the <code>And</code> or <code>Or</code> operators. Each condition consists of a property path, an operator, and a value.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="single-operand-condition">Single operand (condition)<a href="#single-operand-condition" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Single operand (condition)" title="Direct link to Single operand (condition)" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>Each set of algebraic conditions is called an &quot;operand&quot;. For each operand, the required properties are:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The operator type,</li>
<li class="">The property path, and</li>
<li class="">The value as well as the value type.</li>
</ul>
<p>For example, this filter will only allow objects from the class <code>Article</code> with a <code>wordCount</code> that is <code>GreaterThan</code> than <code>1000</code>.</p>

plain">        path: [\&quot;wordCount\&quot;],</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        operator: GreaterThan,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        valueInt: 1000</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      }) {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        title</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  }&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}&#x27; | curl \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span <details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Expected response</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><div class="language-text <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-structure">Filter structure<a href="#filter-structure" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter structure" title="Direct link to Filter structure" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>The <code>where</code> filter is an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algebraic_structure" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">algebraic object</a>, which takes the following arguments:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>Operator</code> (which takes one of the following values)<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><code>And</code></li>
<li class=""><code>Or</code></li>
<li class=""><code>Not</code></li>
<li class=""><code>Equal</code></li>
<li class=""><code>NotEqual</code></li>
<li class=""><code>GreaterThan</code></li>
<li class=""><code>GreaterThanEqual</code></li>
<li class=""><code>LessThan</code></li>
<li class=""><code>LessThanEqual</code></li>
<li class=""><code>Like</code></li>
<li class=""><code>WithinGeoRange</code></li>
<li class=""><code>IsNull</code></li>
<li class=""><code>ContainsAny</code>  (*Only for array and text properties)</li>
<li class=""><code>ContainsAll</code>  (*Only for array and text properties)</li>
<li class=""><code>ContainsNone</code> (*Only for array and text properties)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class=""><code>Path</code>: Is a list of strings in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XPath#Abbreviated_syntax" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">XPath</a> style, indicating the property name of the collection.<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="">If the property is a cross-reference, the path should be followed as a list of strings. For a <code>inPublication</code> reference property that refers to <code>Publication</code> collection, the path selector for <code>name</code> will be <code>[&quot;inPublication&quot;, &quot;Publication&quot;, &quot;name&quot;]</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class=""><code>valueType</code>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>valueInt</code>: For <code>int</code> data type.</li>
<li class=""><code>valueBoolean</code>: For <code>boolean</code> data type.</li>
<li class=""><code>valueString</code>: For <code>string</code> data type (note: <code>string</code> has been deprecated).</li>
<li class=""><code>valueText</code>: For <code>text</code>, <code>uuid</code>, <code>geoCoordinates</code>, <code>phoneNumber</code> data types.</li>
<li class=""><code>valueNumber</code>: For <code>number</code> data type.</li>
<li class=""><code>valueDate</code>: For <code>date</code> (ISO 8601 timestamp, formatted as <a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc3339/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">RFC3339</a>) data type.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>If the operator is <code>And</code> or <code>Or</code>, the operands are a list of <code>where</code> filters.</p>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Example filter structure (GraphQL)</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-behaviors">Filter behaviors<a href="#filter-behaviors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter behaviors" title="Direct link to Filter behaviors" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="multi-word-queries-in-equal-filters">Multi-word queries in <code>Equal</code> filters<a href="#multi-word-queries-in-equal-filters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to multi-word-queries-in-equal-filters" title="Direct link to multi-word-queries-in-equal-filters" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>The behavior for the <code>Equal</code> operator on multi-word textual properties in <code>where</code> filters depends on the <code>tokenization</code> of the property.</p>
<p>See the <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#tokenization">Schema property tokenization section</a> for the difference between the available tokenization types.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="stopwords-in-text-filters">Stopwords in <code>text</code> filters<a href="#stopwords-in-text-filters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to stopwords-in-text-filters" title="Direct link to stopwords-in-text-filters" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Starting with <code>v1.12.0</code> you can configure your own <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/indexing/inverted-index#stopwords">stopword lists for the inverted index</a>.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="multiple-operands">Multiple operands<a href="#multiple-operands" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multiple operands" title="Direct link to Multiple operands" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<p>You can set multiple operands or <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/filters#nested-filters">nest conditions</a>.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>You can filter datetimes similarly to numbers, with the <code>valueDate</code> given as <code>string</code> in <a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc3339/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">RFC3339</a> format.</p></div></div>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-operators">Filter operators<a href="#filter-operators" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter operators" title="Direct link to Filter operators" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="like"><code>Like</code><a href="#like" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to like" title="Direct link to like" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The <code>Like</code> operator filters <code>text</code> data based on partial matches. It can be used with the following wildcard characters:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>?</code> -&gt; exactly one unknown character<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><code>car?</code> matches <code>cart</code>, <code>care</code>, but not <code>car</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class=""><code>*</code> -&gt; zero, one or more unknown characters<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><code>car*</code> matches <code>car</code>, <code>care</code>, <code>carpet</code>, etc</li>
<li class=""><code>*car*</code> matches <code>car</code>, <code>healthcare</code>, etc.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<!-- -->

style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;Publication&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;The New York Times Company&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;International New York Times&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;New York Times&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;New Yorker&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></details>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="performance-of-like">Performance of <code>Like</code><a href="#performance-of-like" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to performance-of-like" title="Direct link to performance-of-like" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Each <code>Like</code> filter iterates over the entire inverted index for that property. The search time will go up linearly with the dataset size, and may become slow for large datasets.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="wildcard-literal-matches-with-like">Wildcard literal matches with <code>Like</code><a href="#wildcard-literal-matches-with-like" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to wildcard-literal-matches-with-like" title="Direct link to wildcard-literal-matches-with-like" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p>Currently, the <code>Like</code> filter is not able to match wildcard characters (<code>?</code> and <code>*</code>) as literal characters. For example, it is currently not possible to only match the string <code>car*</code> and not <code>car</code>, <code>care</code> or <code>carpet</code>. This is a known limitation and may be addressed in future versions of Weaviate.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="containsany--containsall--containsnone"><code>ContainsAny</code> / <code>ContainsAll</code> / <code>ContainsNone</code><a href="#containsany--containsall--containsnone" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to containsany--containsall--containsnone" title="Direct link to containsany--containsall--containsnone" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>The <code>ContainsAny</code>, <code>ContainsAll</code> and <code>ContainsNone</code> operators filter objects using values of an array as criteria.</p>
<p>Both operators expect an array of values and return objects that match based on the input values.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span><code>ContainsAny</code>/<code>ContainsAll</code>/<code>ContainsNone</code> notes:</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><ul>
<li class="">The <code>ContainsAny</code>, <code>ContainsAll</code> and <code>ContainsNone</code> operators treat texts as an array. The text is split into an array of tokens based on the chosen tokenization scheme, and the search is performed on that array.</li>
<li class="">When using <code>ContainsAny</code>, <code>ContainsAll</code> and <code>ContainsNone</code> with the REST api for <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-objects/delete#delete-multiple-objects">batch deletion</a>, the text array must be specified with the <code>valueTextArray</code> argument. This is different from the usage in search, where the <code>valueText</code> argument that can be used.</li>
</ul></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="containsany"><code>ContainsAny</code><a href="#containsany" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to containsany" title="Direct link to containsany" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p><code>ContainsAny</code> returns objects where at least one of the values from the input array is present.</p>
<p>Consider a dataset of <code>Person</code>, where each object represents a person with a <code>languages_spoken</code> property with a <code>text</code> datatype.</p>
<p>A <code>ContainsAny</code> query on a path of <code>[&quot;languages_spoken&quot;]</code> with a value of <code>[&quot;Chinese&quot;, &quot;French&quot;, &quot;English&quot;]</code> will return objects where at least one of those languages is present in the <code>languages_spoken</code> array.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="containsall"><code>ContainsAll</code><a href="#containsall" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to containsall" title="Direct link to containsall" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p><code>ContainsAll</code> returns objects where all the values from the input array are present.</p>
<p>Using the same dataset of <code>Person</code> objects as above, a <code>ContainsAll</code> query on a path of <code>[&quot;languages_spoken&quot;]</code> with a value of <code>[&quot;Chinese&quot;, &quot;French&quot;, &quot;English&quot;]</code> will return objects where all three of those languages are present in the <code>languages_spoken</code> array.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="containsnone"><code>ContainsNone</code><a href="#containsnone" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to containsnone" title="Direct link to containsnone" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<p><code>ContainsNone</code> returns objects where none of the values from the input array are present.</p>
<p>Using the same dataset of <code>Person</code> objects as above, a <code>ContainsNone</code> query on a path of <code>[&quot;languages_spoken&quot;]</code> with a value of <code>[&quot;Chinese&quot;, &quot;French&quot;, &quot;English&quot;]</code> will return objects where <strong>none</strong> of those languages are present in the <code>languages_spoken</code> array. For example, a person who speaks only Spanish would be returned, but a person who speaks English would be excluded.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-performance">Filter performance<a href="#filter-performance" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter performance" title="Direct link to Filter performance" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<p>In some edge cases, filter performance may be slow due to a mismatch between the filter architecture and the data structure. For example, if a property has very large cardinality (i.e. a large number of unique values), its range-based filter performance may be slow.</p>
<p>If you are experiencing slow filter performance, you have several options:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Further restrict your query by adding more conditions to the <code>where</code> operator</li>
<li class="">Add a <code>limit</code> parameter to your query</li>
<li class="">Configure <code>indexRangeFilters</code> for properties that require range-based filtering. You can <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/inverted-index">set inverted index parameters</a> when creating your collection. Learn more about <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/indexing/inverted-index#configure-inverted-indexes">configuring the inverted index</a> to optimize filter performance for your specific use case.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="special-cases">Special cases<a href="#special-cases" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Special cases" title="Direct link to Special cases" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-id">By id<a href="#by-id" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By id" title="Direct link to By id" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>You can filter object by their unique id or uuid, where you give the <code>id</code> as <code>valueText</code>.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-timestamps">By timestamps<a href="#by-timestamps" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By timestamps" title="Direct link to By timestamps" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Filtering can be performed with internal timestamps as well, such as <code>creationTimeUnix</code> and <code>lastUpdateTimeUnix</code>. These values can be represented either as Unix epoch milliseconds, or as <a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc3339/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">RFC3339</a> formatted datetimes. Note that epoch milliseconds should be passed in as a <code>valueText</code>, and an RFC3339 datetime should be a <code>valueDate</code>.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Filtering by timestamp requires the target class to be configured to index  timestamps. See <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/indexing/inverted-index#indextimestamps">here</a> for details.</p></div></div>

style="color:#36acaa">&quot;title&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Army builds new body armor 14-times stronger in the face of enemy fire&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        ...</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></details>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-property-length">By property length<a href="#by-property-length" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By property length" title="Direct link to By property length" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Filtering can be performed with the length of properties.</p>
<p>The length of properties is calculated differently depending on the type:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">array types: the number of entries in the array is used, where null (property not present) and empty arrays both have the length 0.</li>
<li class="">strings and texts: the number of characters (unicode characters such as ä¸– count as one character).</li>
<li class="">numbers, booleans, geo-coordinates, phone-numbers and data-blobs are not supported.</li>
</ul>
<div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token object">Get</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">Class</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">where</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">operator</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">Operator</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">valueInt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">value</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">path</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;len(&lt;property&gt;)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Supported operators are <code>(not) equal</code> and <code>greater/less than (equal)</code> and values need to be 0 or larger.</p>
<p>Note that the <code>path</code> value is a string, where the property name is wrapped in <code>len()</code>. For example, to filter for objects based on the length of the <code>title</code> property, you would use <code>path: [&quot;len(title)&quot;]</code>.</p>
<p>To filter for <code>Article</code> class objects with <code>title</code> length greater than 10, you would use:</p>
<div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token object">Get</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token property-query">Article</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">where</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">operator</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token class-name">GreaterThan</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">valueInt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">10</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">path</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;len(title)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Filtering by property length requires the target class to be <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/indexing/inverted-index#indexpropertylength">configured to index the length</a>.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-cross-references">By cross-references<a href="#by-cross-references" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By cross-references" title="Direct link to By cross-references" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>You can also search for the value of the property of a cross-references, also called beacons.</p>
<p>For example, these filters select based on the class Article but who have <code>inPublication</code> set to New Yorker.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-count-of-reference">By count of reference<a href="#by-count-of-reference" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By count of reference" title="Direct link to By count of reference" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Above example shows how filter by reference can solve straightforward questions like &quot;Find all articles that are published by New Yorker&quot;. But questions like &quot;Find all articles that are written by authors that wrote at least two articles&quot;, cannot be answered by the above query structure. It is however possible to filter by reference count. To do so, simply provide one of the existing compare operators (<code>Equal</code>, <code>LessThan</code>, <code>LessThanEqual</code>, <code>GreaterThan</code>, <code>GreaterThanEqual</code>) and use it directly on the reference element. For example:</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-geo-coordinates">By geo coordinates<a href="#by-geo-coordinates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By geo coordinates" title="Direct link to By geo coordinates" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>A special case of the <code>Where</code> filter is with geoCoordinates. This filter is only supported by the <code>Get{}</code> function. If you&#x27;ve set the <code>geoCoordinates</code> property type, you can search in an area based on kilometers.</p>
<p>For example, this curious returns all in a radius of 2KM around a specific geo-location:</p>

style="color:#36acaa">&quot;headquartersGeoLocation&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;latitude&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">51.512737</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;longitude&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-0.0962234</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;International New York Times&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></details>
<p>Note that <code>geoCoordinates</code> uses a vector index under the hood.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>Limitations</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Currently, geo-coordinate filtering is limited to the nearest 800 results from the source location, which will be further reduced by any other filter conditions and search parameters.</p><p>If you plan on a densely populated dataset, consider using another strategy such as geo-hashing into a <code>text</code> datatype, and filtering further, such as with a <code>ContainsAny</code> filter.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="by-null-state">By null state<a href="#by-null-state" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to By null state" title="Direct link to By null state" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Using the <code>IsNull</code> operator allows you to do filter for objects where given properties are <code>null</code> or <code>not null</code>. Note that zero-length arrays and empty strings are equivalent to a null value.</p>
<div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token object">Get</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">Class</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">where</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">operator</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token class-name">IsNull</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">valueBoolean</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> &lt;</span><span class="token boolean" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain">/</span><span class="token boolean" style="color:#36acaa">false</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">path</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token plain">&lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">property</span><span class="token plain">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Filtering by null-state requires the target class to be configured to index this. See <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/indexing/inverted-index#indexnullstate">here</a> for details.</p></div></div>
